	QIE_establish_rk_ALB = {
		icon = generic_prepare_civil_war
	
			highlight_states = {
				highlight_state_targets = {
					state = 44
					state = 1268
				}
				highlight_color_while_active = 3
				highlight_color_before_active = 2
			}
	
		available = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					ALB = { exists = yes }
				}
				ALB = { is_subject_of = QIE }
			}
			44 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = QIE is_subject_of = QIE } } }
			1268 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = QIE is_subject_of = QIE } } }
			OR = {
					44 = { NOT = { is_core_of = QIE } }
					1268 = { NOT = { is_core_of = QIE } }
			}
		}
	
		fire_only_once = yes
	
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 5
		}
		complete_effect = {
			ALB = {
				every_core_state = {
					remove_core_of = ALB
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_claimed_by = ALB
					}
					remove_claim_by = ALB
				}
			}
			44 = { add_core_of = ALB }
			1268 = { add_core_of = ALB }
			release = ALB
			ALB = { 
				every_core_state = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { 
								is_core_of = QIE
							}
							OR = {
								is_owned_by = QIE
								OWNER = { is_subject_of = QIE} 
							}
						}
					}
					transfer_state_to = ALB
				}
			}
			ALB = { 
				set_cosmetic_tag = QIE_ALB_OCC
				load_focus_tree = generic_focus            
	
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Qing Royal Administration"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/WDQIE/qing_administration.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = autocratic_colonial_govt_subtype
					traits = {
					}
				}	
	
				QIE = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = ALB
						autonomous_state = kx_colored_puppet
					}
				}
	
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
					elections_allowed = no
				}
	
	
				set_popularities = {
					syndicalist = 5
					social_democrat = 5
					social_liberal = 0
					market_liberal = 0
					social_conservative = 20
					authoritarian_democrat = 50
					paternal_autocrat = 10
					national_populist = 10
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = paternal_autocrat
					name = "Qing Royal Administration"
					long_name = "Qing Royal Administration"
				}
	
			}
		}


	}

			highlight_states = {
				highlight_state_targets = {
					state = 122
					state = 1225
				}
				highlight_color_while_active = 3
				highlight_color_before_active = 2
			}

		available = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					WAL = { exists = yes }
				}
				WAL = { is_subject_of = QIE }
			}
			122 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = QIE is_subject_of = QIE } } }
			1225 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = QIE is_subject_of = QIE } } }
			OR = {
					122 = { NOT = { is_core_of = QIE } }
					1225 = { NOT = { is_core_of = QIE } }
			}
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 5
		}
		complete_effect = {
			WAL = {
				every_core_state = {
					remove_core_of = WAL
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_claimed_by = WAL
					}
					remove_claim_by = WAL
				}
			}
			122 = { add_core_of = WAL }
			1225 = { add_core_of = WAL }
			release = WAL
			WAL = { 
				every_core_state = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { 
								is_core_of = QIE
							}
							OR = {
								is_owned_by = QIE
								OWNER = { is_subject_of = QIE} 
							}
						}
					}
					transfer_state_to = WAL
				}
			}
			WAL = { 
				set_cosmetic_tag = QIE_WAL_OCC
				load_focus_tree = generic_focus            
	
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Qing Royal Administration"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/WDQIE/qing_administration.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = autocratic_colonial_govt_subtype
					traits = {
					}
				}

				QIE = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = WAL
						autonomous_state = kx_colored_puppet
					}
				}

				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
					elections_allowed = no
				}


				set_popularities = {
					syndicalist = 5
					social_democrat = 5
					social_liberal = 0
					market_liberal = 0
					social_conservative = 20
					authoritarian_democrat = 50
					paternal_autocrat = 10
					national_populist = 10
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = paternal_autocrat
					name = "Qing Royal Administration"
					long_name = "Qing Royal Administration"
				}

			}
		}
	}
